1575423156--SELECT online.assist_prd,online.cus_no,b.cus_name,
		case when online.prd_sku_id != '' then b.qty else ifnull(a.qty,0) end  as qty,
		case when online.prd_sku_id != '' then (case when z.prd_sku_id = online.prd_sku_id then '已绑定' else '未绑定' end) else (case when product.prd_id = online.prd_id then '已绑定' else '未绑定' end) end  as binding,
		online.id AS on_id,online.outer_iid AS outer_iid,online.shopid AS on_shopid,online.title AS on_title,online.pic AS on_pic,online.outer_iid AS on_outer_id,online.have_sku,online.num_iid as on_num_iid,
				product.id AS sys_id,product.prd_no AS sys_prd_no,product.title AS sys_title,product.pic_path AS sys_pic,online.prd_id,online.replace_prd_no,
				online.cid_name,online.goods_no,online.brand,online.material,online.material_in,online.standard,online.security,online.retailPrice,online.addtime,online.num_iid,online.cost_price,online.stalls_no  
				FROM u13123456789_product_online AS online 
				LEFT JOIN u13123456789_product AS product ON product.prd_id = online.prd_id 
				LEFT JOIN (select prd_id,sum(qty) as qty from u13123456789_prdt_wms_qty group by prd_id) as a on a.prd_id = online.prd_id
				LEFT JOIN (select prd_sku_id,sum(qty) as qty from u13123456789_prdt_wms_qty where prd_sku_id<>'' group by prd_sku_id) as b on b.prd_sku_id = online.prd_sku_id
				LEFT JOIN u13123456789_cust b on online.cus_no=b.cus_no 
				LEFT JOIN(select prd_id,prd_sku_id from u13123456789_product_sku) z on z.prd_sku_id = online.prd_sku_id
				
				WHERE 1 AND online.shopid = 'shuaibao-1' 
				ORDER BY online.id  ASC limit 0,20
